posted:Posted May 8, 2024
msg:"Wanda Yihua Hotel, Chengdu"
After the music festival, I thought that since I was here, I had to go to the city center to have a look. So after careful selection, I decided to book this Wanda Yihua Hotel.

This is my first time staying in a Wanda hotel. The overall experience is quite good. The hotel is located near Donghu Park. Although it is close to the Second Ring Road, the interior is very quiet, and it has a sense of tranquility in the bustle. The decoration incorporates oriental Bashu elements. Wanda Yihua Hotel is positioned as a hotel that pursues comfort and livability while also having a sense of design and a high-end lifestyle. Relatively speaking, it is more suitable for young people to stay.

I arrived late that day, around twelve o'clock, and the front desk checked in very quickly. Each room is equipped with two room cards, one of which should be an electric card. The design of the card is quite interesting, and the print is in the style of a tape.
The room has a double-basin washbasin, and the bathtub is also equipped with a disposable bath bag, bath salt ball and a small bath flower ball, which is very considerate. However, the hygiene of the carpet in the room needs more attention, and some places are still obviously dirty.

Sleep until dawn and see how the breakfast of the Wanda Hotel is made. The breakfast variety is not rich, but there is nothing missing. There are freshly made special tofu, small noodles, wontons and Lai Tangyuan. The supply of breakfast is always updated, and the food is added very quickly.

Before leaving, I originally planned not to go to the lobby and check out directly by phone. But the handsome guy at the front desk said that he prepared a souvenir for us. Later, I found out that it was some snacks when I got on the car. Although the price is not high, this thought is a good plus point. It can be felt that the hotel's service is still attentive.
